The API handler calls `Service.Upsert()` which stores to database and calls registered reloadables\\n  2. Each reloadable's `Reload()` method is invoked with the new settings\\n  3. OAuth connectors update their internal configuration in-memory\\n  4. Subsequent authentication requests use the new configuration immediately\\n  5. Fallback strategies allow reading legacy configurations during the migration period\\n\\n## Security and Audit Trail\\n\\n1. **Feature Flag Gating**: The flag prevents unauthorized access to the entire SSO settings infrastructure when not enabled\\n2. **Access Control Scopes**: Providers are individually scoped (e.g., `settings:auth:google:*`), preventing privilege escalation\\n3. **Audit Trail**: Access control logs all changes through the middleware; secrets are encrypted at rest\\n4. **Validation Pipeline**: Each connector validates new settings before accepting them, with requester identity passed through\\n5. **Backwards Compatibility**: Fallback strategies allow gradual migration from file-based to API-based configuration\\n\\nThis architecture ensures that the SSO settings control is properly enforced end-to-end: feature-flagged at definition, conditionally initialized in the service layer, access-controlled at the API layer, and restricted in the UI, creating multiple layers of protection for sensitive OAuth configuration.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":858,"cache_read_input_tokens":73317,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":858},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"dfd9c5aa-3474-4ddc-9a98-c30c67017122","uuid":"db2e503e-4d97-44ad-a966-7144dd301c2c"}

Reloadable management: Maps providers to their Reloadable implementations for live configuration updates\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettingsimpl/metrics.go**: Prometheus metrics for tracking reload failures and other operational metrics.\\n\\n### Fallback Strategies for Backwards Compatibility:\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ssosettings/strategies/oauth_strategy.go**: Implements `FallbackStrategy` to load OAuth settings from config files/environment\\n- **pkg/services/ssosettings/strategies/ldap_strategy.go**: Implements `FallbackStrategy` for LDAP settings\\n- **pkg/services/ssosettings/strategies/saml_strategy.go**: Implements `FallbackStrategy` for SAML settings (when licensed)\\n\\n### Database Migrations:\\n\\n- **pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ssosettings/migrations.go**: Defines the `sso_setting` table migration with columns for id (primary key), provider, settings (JSON), created, updated, and is_deleted timestamps.\\n\\n## Layer 3: API & Authentication Wiring\\n\\nThis layer implements the REST API endpoints and wires OAuth connectors to the SSO settings service:\\n\\n### REST API Endpoints:\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ssosettings/api/api.go**: Implements the HTTP API with:\\n  - `RegisterAPIEndpoints()`: Creates the `/api/v1/sso-settings` route group with four endpoints:\\n    - `GET /api/v1/sso-settings`: List all provider settings (requires `ActionSettingsRead`)\\n    - `GET /api/v1/sso-settings/:key`: Get settings for a specific provider (requires `ActionSettingsRead` with provider scope)\\n    - `PUT /api/v1/sso-settings/:key`: Update provider settings (requires `ActionSettingsWrite` with provider scope)\\n    - `DELETE /api/v1/sso-settings/:key`: Delete provider settings (requires `ActionSettingsWrite` with provider scope)\\n  - Each endpoint is protected by access control middleware checking specific scopes (e.g., `ScopeSettingsOAuth`)\\n  - Responses include ETag-based HTTP caching for efficiency\\n\\n- **pkg/api/api.go**: Integrates SSO settings API routes into the main Grafana router. Access control evaluators determine who can access these routes.\\n\\n### OAuth Connector Registration:\\n\\nMultiple OAuth connectors implement the `Reloadable` interface and register themselves with the SSO settings service when the feature flag is enabled:\\n\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/google_oauth.go**: Google connector registers via `ssoSettings.RegisterReloadable(social.GoogleProviderName, provider)` (lines 60-63)\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/gitlab_oauth.go**: GitLab connector registration (lines 60-63)\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/okta_oauth.go**: Okta connector registration (lines 56-60)\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/github_oauth.go**: GitHub connector registration (lines 78-81)\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/grafana_com_oauth.go**: Grafana.com connector registration (lines 50-53)\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/generic_oauth.go**: Generic OAuth connector registration (lines 71-73)\\n- **pkg/login/social/connectors/azuread_oauth.go**: Azure AD connector registration (lines 92-95)\\n\\nEach connector implements `Reload()` and `Validate()` methods to respond to configuration changes from the SSO settings API.\\n\\n### Social Service Provider:\\n\\n- **pkg/login/social/socialimpl/service.go**: The `SocialService` initializes OAuth connectors. The API handler calls `Service.Upsert()` which stores to database and calls registered reloadables\\n  2. Each reloadable's `Reload()` method is invoked with the new settings\\n  3. OAuth connectors update their internal configuration in-memory\\n  4. Subsequent authentication requests use the new configuration immediately\\n  5. Fallback strategies allow reading legacy configurations during the migration period\\n\\n## Security and Audit Trail\\n\\n1. **Feature Flag Gating**: The flag prevents unauthorized access to the entire SSO settings infrastructure when not enabled\\n2. **Access Control Scopes**: Providers are individually scoped (e.g., `settings:auth:google:*`), preventing privilege escalation\\n3. **Audit Trail**: Access control logs all changes through the middleware; secrets are encrypted at rest\\n4. **Validation Pipeline**: Each connector validates new settings before accepting them, with requester identity passed through\\n5. **Backwards Compatibility**: Fallback strategies allow gradual migration from file-based to API-based configuration\\n\\nThis architecture ensures that the SSO settings control is properly enforced end-to-end: feature-flagged at definition, conditionally initialized in the service layer, access-controlled at the API layer, and restricted in the UI, creating multiple layers of protection for sensitive OAuth configuration.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
